               <div class="hideit" itemprop="image" itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject"> 
                <meta content="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qJXY9cQJRBE/VrETOipv_KI/AAAAAAAAC_g/iw_qRHp5nQ8/s400/quickSort.png" itemprop="url">

               <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7667313618893411705" itemprop="articleBody"> 
                <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on"> 
                 <h2> Quick sort algorithm implementation in java</h2> As the name, quick sort is the most quick algorithm to sort some number. There are some other sorting algorithm like 
                 <a href="http://programminghelpbd.blogspot.com/2015/03/bucket-sort-algorithm-implementation.html" target="_blank"><b>bucket sort</b></a>, insertion sort, 
                 <a href="http://programminghelpbd.blogspot.com/2014/06/bubble-sort-in-java.html" target="_blank">bubble sort</a>, 
                 <a href="http://programminghelpbd.blogspot.com/2015/03/radix-sort-algorithm-implementation-in-c.html" target="_blank">radix sort</a> etc. Among them, quick sort is very efficient.
                 <br> Here is the step diagram of quick sort:
                 <br> 
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"> 
                  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qJXY9cQJRBE/VrETOipv_KI/AAAAAAAAC_g/iw_qRHp5nQ8/s1600/quickSort.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="308" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qJXY9cQJRBE/VrETOipv_KI/AAAAAAAAC_g/iw_qRHp5nQ8/s400/quickSort.png" width="400"></a>
                 </div> Let's look at the code:
                 <br> 
                 <a name="more"></a>
                 <br> 
                 <a href="https://www.blogger.com/blogger.g?blogID=6995178116588215115" name="more"></a> 
                 <textarea cols="80" rows="25" wrap="hard">import java.util.Scanner ;
 public class MyQuick {
  private int ar[] ;
  private int length ;
  private static Scanner w ;
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    w = new Scanner(System.in) ;
    int i,n ;
    System.out.println("Numbers of elements : ");
    n = w.nextInt() ;
    int [] a = new int [n] ;
    System.out.println("Elements are : ");
    for(i = 0; i &lt; n; i++)
    {
     a[i] = w.nextInt() ;
         }
    MyQuick quick = new MyQuick () ;
    quick.Sort(a) ;
    System.out.println("After sorting the elements are :");
    for(int q : a)    {
      System.out.println(q);
    }
  }
  public void Sort(int [] a)
  {
   this.ar = a ;
   this.length = a.length ;
   QuickSort(0,length - 1) ;
   if(ar == null || ar.length == 0)
   {
    return ;
   }
  }
  private void QuickSort(int low, int high)  {
   int i = low ;
   int j = high ;   //calculate pivot number , i m talking pivot as middle index number
   int pivot = ar [low + (high - low) / 2] ;   //divide into two arrays
   while(i &lt;= j)
   {
    while(ar[i] &lt; pivot)
    {
     i++ ;
    }
    while(ar[j] &gt; pivot)
    {
     j-- ;
    }
    if(i &lt;= j)
    {
     Exchange(i,j) ;
     //move index to nest position on both sides
     i++ ;
     j-- ;
    }
   }
   //call quicksort method recursively
   if(low &lt; j)
   {
    QuickSort(low,j) ;
   }
   if(i &lt; high)
   {
    QuickSort(i,high) ;
   }
  }
  private void Exchange(int i, int j)
  {
   int temp = ar[i];
   ar[i] = ar[j] ;
   ar[j] = temp ;
  }
     }
   </textarea>
                 <br> 
                 <br> Happy Coding...
